  - paragraph:
    - text: This is a list of every
    - link "One Piece":
      - /url: /wiki/One_Piece_(Manga)
    - text: character that has ever appeared in or been mentioned in the
    - link "manga":
      - /url: /wiki/One_Piece_(Manga)

    - text: or an

      - /url: /wiki/SBS

    - link "animals":

    - text: ","
    - link "zombies":
      - /url: /wiki/Zombie
    - text: and numbered groups of unnamed people. Note that some names have
    - link "alternate spellings":
      - /url: /wiki/Name_Variants
    - text: ", which are not included on this list."
